for post-punk bands playing music in 2017. Fronted by Ian McCulloch, the Bunnymen emerged with debut album Crocodiles and quickly became a cornerstone of teen punks’ record collections circa 1980. (To be fair, the act didn’t just fade away once the ’90s rolled around. The 1984 single “The Killing Moon” is not only timeless, but integral to understanding the development of the genre.) Thirty years and one fatal motorcycle accident, breakup and subsequent reunion later, Echo and the Bunnymen are still proving their mettle. McCulloch and guitarist Will Sergeant are the only remaining members of the original lineup, and it’s highly likely that they’ll play the hits when they come to Denver.
